I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
BUG: 'setup-cli' action referenced by mutable tag instead of commit SHA in maintenance workflow
## Summary

The `agentics-maintenance.yml` workflow compiled by gh-aw v0.64.0 references `github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli` using the mutable tag `@v0.64.0` rather than a pinned full commit SHA. Every other action in this repo (and in `copilot-setup-steps.yml`) is pinned to a commit SHA for supply-chain integrity and reproducibility. This inconsistency weakens the security posture of the workflow.

### What failed
- `uses: github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@v0.64.0` — mutable tag, not a SHA pin.
- All other action references in the same repository use SHA-pinned references.

### Why it failed
- The compiler's action pinning logic (via `GetActionPin()` and `.github/aw/actions-lock.json`) did not resolve and emit the commit SHA for `setup-cli` in the context of the maintenance workflow generation.

### Root cause
- Gap in the action pinning/lock resolution logic in the compiler when generating maintenance workflow references to `setup-cli`.
- The correct SHA is known (`51c65948c64ab6752536ead71fba1fc2c20ed0bc`) and is used elsewhere; it simply wasn't applied here.

### Supporting evidence / References
- [PR Review Copilot observation 11](https://github.com/grahame-org/gnu-tools-for-stm32/pull/682#pullrequestreview-4013076953)
- Compiler pinning code: `GetActionPin()` and `.github/aw/actions-lock.json`
- Example of correct SHA pinning in `copilot-setup-steps.yml` in same repo

### Proposed fix
- Ensure `GetActionPin()` (or equivalent) correctly resolves and emits the SHA for `setup-cli` in all compiler code paths, including maintenance workflow generation.
- The suggestion from review: `uses: github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@51c65948c64ab6752536ead71fba1fc2c20ed0bc # v0.64.0`
- Add a compiler test asserting that all emitted action references are SHA-pinned (no bare tags).

### Implementation plan
1. Audit compiler workflow generators for any `setup-cli` or other action references that bypass the `GetActionPin()` / `actions-lock.json` resolution path.
2. Fix the identified code path to use the SHA from the lock.
3. Add a test asserting no mutable tag references in any compiled `.lock.yml` output.


</pr_description>

    15	// generateInstallCLISteps generates YAML steps to install or build the gh-aw CLI.
    16	// In dev mode: builds from source using Setup Go + Build gh-aw (./gh-aw binary available)
    17	// In release mode: installs the released CLI via the setup-cli action (gh aw available)
    18	// In action mode: installs the released CLI via the gh-aw-actions/setup-cli action (gh aw available)
    19	func generateInstallCLISteps(actionMode ActionMode, version string, actionTag string) string {
    20	        if actionMode == ActionModeDev {
    21	                return `      - name: Setup Go
    22	        uses: ` + GetActionPin("actions/setup-go") + `
    23	        with:
    24	          go-version-file: go.mod
    25	          cache: true
    26	
    27	      - name: Build gh-aw
    28	        run: make build
    29	
    30	`
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        cliTag := actionTag
    34	        if cliTag == "" {
    35	                cliTag = version
    36	        }
    37	
    38	        // Action mode: use setup-cli action from external gh-aw-actions repository
    39	        if actionMode == ActionModeAction {
    40	                return `      - name: Install gh-aw
    41	        uses: github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@` + cliTag + `
    42	        with:
    43	          version: ` + cliTag + `
    44	
    45	`
    46	        }
    47	
    48	        // Release mode: use setup-cli action (consistent with copilot-setup-steps.yml)
    49	        return `      - name: Install gh-aw
    50	        uses: github/gh-aw/actions/setup-cli@` + cliTag + `
    51	        with:
    52	          version: ` + cliTag + `
    53	
    54	`
    55	}

    57	// getCLICmdPrefix returns the CLI command prefix based on action mode.
    58	// In dev mode: "./gh-aw" (local binary built from source)
    59	// In release mode: "gh aw" (installed via gh extension)
    60	func getCLICmdPrefix(actionMode ActionMode) string {
    61	        if actionMode == ActionModeDev {
    62	                return "./gh-aw"
    63	        }
    64	        return "gh aw"
    65	}

    67	// generateMaintenanceCron generates a cron schedule based on the minimum expires value in days
    68	// Schedule runs at minimum required frequency to check expirations at appropriate intervals
    69	// Returns cron expression and description.
    70	func generateMaintenanceCron(minExpiresDays int) (string, string) {
    71	        // Use a pseudo-random but deterministic minute (37) to avoid load spikes at :00
    72	        minute := 37
    73	
    74	        // Determine frequency based on minimum expires value (in days)
    75	        // Run at least as often as the shortest expiration would need
    76	        if minExpiresDays <= 1 {
    77	                // For 1 day or less, run every 2 hours
    78	                return fmt.Sprintf("%d */2 * * *", minute), "Every 2 hours"
    79	        } else if minExpiresDays == 2 {
    80	                // For 2 days, run every 6 hours
    81	                return fmt.Sprintf("%d */6 * * *", minute), "Every 6 hours"
    82	        } else if minExpiresDays <= 4 {
    83	                // For 3-4 days, run every 12 hours
    84	                return fmt.Sprintf("%d */12 * * *", minute), "Every 12 hours"
    85	        }
    86	
    87	        // For more than 4 days, run daily
    88	        return fmt.Sprintf("%d %d * * *", minute, 0), "Daily"
    89	}

    17	var actionPinsLog = logger.New("workflow:action_pins")
    18	
    19	//go:embed data/action_pins.json
    20	var actionPinsJSON []byte
    21	
    22	// formatActionReference formats an action reference with repo, SHA, and version.
    23	// Example: "actions/checkout@abc123 # v4.1.0"
    24	func formatActionReference(repo, sha, version string) string {
    25	        return fmt.Sprintf("%s@%s # %s", repo, sha, version)
    26	}
    27	
    28	// formatActionCacheKey generates a cache key for action resolution.
    29	// Example: "actions/checkout@v4"
    30	func formatActionCacheKey(repo, version string) string {
    31	        return fmt.Sprintf("%s@%s", repo, version)
    32	}
    33	
    34	// ActionPin represents a pinned GitHub Action with its commit SHA
    35	type ActionPin struct {
    36	        Repo    string                      `json:"repo"`             // e.g., "actions/checkout"
    37	        Version string                      `json:"version"`          // e.g., "v5" - the golden/default version
    38	        SHA     string                      `json:"sha"`              // Full commit SHA for the pinned version
    39	        Inputs  map[string]*ActionYAMLInput `json:"inputs,omitempty"` // optional cached inputs (not used for SHA pinning)
    40	}
    41	
    42	// ActionPinsData represents the structure of the embedded JSON file
    43	// This matches the schema used by ActionCache for consistency
    44	type ActionPinsData struct {
    45	        Entries map[string]ActionPin `json:"entries"` // key: "repo@version"
    46	}
    47	
    48	var (
    49	        // cachedActionPins holds the parsed and sorted action pins
    50	        cachedActionPins []ActionPin
    51	        // actionPinsOnce ensures the action pins are loaded only once
    52	        actionPinsOnce sync.Once
    53	)
    54	
    55	// getActionPins returns the action pins from the embedded JSON
    56	// Returns a sorted slice of action pins (by version descending, then by repo name)
    57	// The data is parsed once on first call and cached for subsequent calls
    58	func getActionPins() []ActionPin {
    59	        actionPinsOnce.Do(func() {
    60	                actionPinsLog.Print("Unmarshaling action pins from embedded JSON (first call, will be cached)")
    61	
    62	                var data ActionPinsData
    63	                if err := json.Unmarshal(actionPinsJSON, &data); err != nil {
    64	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Failed to unmarshal action pins JSON: %v", err)
    65	                        panic(fmt.Sprintf("failed to load action pins: %v", err))
    66	                }
    67	
    68	                // Detect and log key/version mismatches
    69	                mismatchCount := 0
    70	                for key, pin := range data.Entries {
    71	                        // Extract version from key (format: "repo@version")
    72	                        if idx := strings.LastIndex(key, "@"); idx != -1 {
    73	                                keyVersion := key[idx+1:]
    74	                                if keyVersion != pin.Version {
    75	                                        mismatchCount++
    76	                                        // Safely truncate SHA for logging
    77	                                        shortSHA := pin.SHA
    78	                                        if len(pin.SHA) > 8 {
    79	                                                shortSHA = pin.SHA[:8]
    80	                                        }
    81	                                        actionPinsLog.Printf("WARNING: Key/version mismatch in action_pins.json: key=%s has version=%s but pin.Version=%s (sha=%s)",
    82	                                                key, keyVersion, pin.Version, shortSHA)
    83	                                }
    84	                        }
    85	                }
    86	                if mismatchCount > 0 {
    87	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Found %d key/version mismatches in action_pins.json", mismatchCount)
    88	                }
    89	
    90	                // Convert map values to slice - immutable initialization
    91	                pins := make([]ActionPin, 0, len(data.Entries))
    92	                for _, pin := range data.Entries {
    93	                        pins = append(pins, pin)
    94	                }
    95	
    96	                // Sort by version (descending) then by repo name (ascending)
    97	                // Use standard library sort for better performance O(n log n) vs O(n²)
    98	                sort.Slice(pins, func(i, j int) bool {
    99	                        // Compare versions first (descending order - higher version first)
   100	                        if pins[i].Version != pins[j].Version {
   101	                                return pins[i].Version > pins[j].Version
   102	                        }
   103	                        // Same version, sort by repo name (ascending order)
   104	                        return pins[i].Repo < pins[j].Repo
   105	                })
   106	
   107	                actionPinsLog.Printf("Successfully unmarshaled and sorted %d action pins from JSON", len(pins))
   108	                cachedActionPins = pins
   109	        })
   110	
   111	        return cachedActionPins
   112	}
   113	
   114	// sortPinsByVersion sorts action pins by version in descending order (highest first).
   115	// This function returns a new sorted slice without modifying the input.
   116	// This is an immutable operation for better safety and clarity.
   117	func sortPinsByVersion(pins []ActionPin) []ActionPin {
   118	        // Create a copy to avoid mutating the input
   119	        result := make([]ActionPin, len(pins))
   120	        copy(result, pins)
   121	
   122	        sort.Slice(result, func(i, j int) bool {
   123	                // Strip 'v' prefix for comparison
   124	                v1 := strings.TrimPrefix(result[i].Version, "v")
   125	                v2 := strings.TrimPrefix(result[j].Version, "v")
   126	                // Return true if v1 > v2 to get descending order
   127	                return compareVersions(v1, v2) > 0
   128	        })
   129	
   130	        return result
   131	}
   132	
   133	// GetActionPin returns the pinned action reference for a given action repository
   134	// When multiple versions exist for the same repo, it returns the latest version by semver
   135	// If no pin is found, it returns an empty string
   136	// The returned reference includes a comment with the version tag (e.g., "repo@sha # v1")
   137	func GetActionPin(actionRepo string) string {
   138	        actionPins := getActionPins()
   139	
   140	        // Find all pins matching the repo - using functional filter
   141	        matchingPins := sliceutil.Filter(actionPins, func(pin ActionPin) bool {
   142	                return pin.Repo == actionRepo
   143	        })
   144	
   145	        if len(matchingPins) == 0 {
   146	                // If no pin exists, return empty string to signal that this action is not pinned
   147	                return ""
   148	        }
   149	
   150	        // Sort matching pins by version (descending - latest first) - immutable operation
   151	        sortedPins := sortPinsByVersion(matchingPins)
   152	
   153	        // Return the latest version (first after sorting)
   154	        latestPin := sortedPins[0]
   155	        return formatActionReference(actionRepo, latestPin.SHA, latestPin.Version)
   156	}
   157	
   158	// GetActionPinWithData returns the pinned action reference for a given action@version
   159	// It tries dynamic resolution first, then falls back to hardcoded pins
   160	// If resolution fails, emits a warning and returns empty string (in both strict and non-strict modes)
   161	// The returned reference includes a comment with the version tag (e.g., "repo@sha # v1")
   162	func GetActionPinWithData(actionRepo, version string, data *WorkflowData) (string, error) {
   163	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Resolving action pin: repo=%s, version=%s, strict_mode=%t", actionRepo, version, data.StrictMode)
   164	
   165	        // Check if version is already a full 40-character SHA
   166	        isAlreadySHA := isValidFullSHA(version)
   167	
   168	        // First try dynamic resolution if resolver is available (but not for SHAs, as they can't be resolved)
   169	        if data.ActionResolver != nil && !isAlreadySHA {
   170	                actionPinsLog.Printf("Attempting dynamic resolution for %s@%s", actionRepo, version)
   171	                sha, err := data.ActionResolver.ResolveSHA(actionRepo, version)
   172	                if err == nil && sha != "" {
   173	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Dynamic resolution succeeded: %s@%s → %s", actionRepo, version, sha)
   174	
   175	                        // Successfully resolved - cache will be saved at end of compilation
   176	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Successfully resolved action pin (cache marked dirty, will save at end)")
   177	                        result := formatActionReference(actionRepo, sha, version)
   178	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Returning pinned reference: %s", result)
   179	                        return result, nil
   180	                }
   181	                actionPinsLog.Printf("Dynamic resolution failed for %s@%s: %v", actionRepo, version, err)
   182	        } else {
   183	                if isAlreadySHA {
   184	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Version is already a SHA, skipping dynamic resolution")
   185	                } else {
   186	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("No action resolver available, skipping dynamic resolution")
   187	                }
   188	        }
   189	
   190	        // Dynamic resolution failed, try hardcoded pins
   191	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Falling back to hardcoded pins for %s@%s", actionRepo, version)
   192	        actionPins := getActionPins()
   193	
   194	        // Find all pins matching the repo - using functional filter
   195	        matchingPins := sliceutil.Filter(actionPins, func(pin ActionPin) bool {
   196	                return pin.Repo == actionRepo
   197	        })
   198	
   199	        if len(matchingPins) == 0 {
   200	                // No pins found for this repo, will handle below
   201	                actionPinsLog.Printf("No hardcoded pins found for %s", actionRepo)
   202	        } else {
   203	                actionPinsLog.Printf("Found %d hardcoded pin(s) for %s", len(matchingPins), actionRepo)
   204	
   205	                // Sort matching pins by version (descending - highest first) - immutable operation
   206	                matchingPins = sortPinsByVersion(matchingPins)
   207	
   208	                // First, try to find an exact version match (for version tags)
   209	                for _, pin := range matchingPins {
   210	                        if pin.Version == version {
   211	                                actionPinsLog.Printf("Exact version match: requested=%s, found=%s", version, pin.Version)
   212	                                return formatActionReference(actionRepo, pin.SHA, pin.Version), nil
   213	                        }
   214	                }
   215	
   216	                // If version is a SHA, check if it matches any hardcoded pin's SHA
   217	                if isAlreadySHA {
   218	                        for _, pin := range matchingPins {
   219	                                if pin.SHA == version {
   220	                                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Exact SHA match: requested=%s, found version=%s", version, pin.Version)
   221	                                        return formatActionReference(actionRepo, pin.SHA, pin.Version), nil
   222	                                }
   223	                        }
   224	                        // SHA provided but doesn't match any hardcoded pin - return it as-is without warnings
   225	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("SHA %s not found in hardcoded pins, returning as-is", version)
   226	                        return formatActionReference(actionRepo, version, version), nil
   227	                }
   228	
   229	                // No exact match found
   230	                // In non-strict mode, find the highest semver-compatible version
   231	                // Semver compatibility means respecting major version boundaries
   232	                // (e.g., v5 -> highest v5.x.x, not v6.x.x)
   233	                if !data.StrictMode && len(matchingPins) > 0 {
   234	                        // Filter for semver-compatible pins (matching major version) - using functional filter
   235	                        compatiblePins := sliceutil.Filter(matchingPins, func(pin ActionPin) bool {
   236	                                return isSemverCompatible(pin.Version, version)
   237	                        })
   238	
   239	                        // If we found compatible pins, use the highest one (first after sorting)
   240	                        // Otherwise fall back to the highest overall pin

   307	// ApplyActionPinToTypedStep applies SHA pinning to a WorkflowStep if it uses an action.
   308	// Returns a modified copy of the step with pinned references.
   309	// If the step doesn't use an action or the action is not pinned, returns the original step.
   310	func ApplyActionPinToTypedStep(step *WorkflowStep, data *WorkflowData) *WorkflowStep {
   311	        // Check if step uses an action
   312	        if step == nil || !step.IsUsesStep() {
   313	                return step
   314	        }
   315	
   316	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Applying action pin to step: uses=%s", step.Uses)
   317	
   318	        // Extract action repo and version from uses field
   319	        actionRepo := extractActionRepo(step.Uses)
   320	        if actionRepo == "" {
   321	                return step
   322	        }
   323	
   324	        version := extractActionVersion(step.Uses)
   325	        if version == "" {
   326	                // No version specified, can't pin
   327	                return step
   328	        }
   329	
   330	        // Try to get pinned SHA
   331	        pinnedRef, err := GetActionPinWithData(actionRepo, version, data)
   332	        if err != nil {
   333	                // In strict mode, this would have already been handled by GetActionPinWithData
   334	                // In normal mode, we just return the original step
   335	                return step
   336	        }
   337	
   338	        if pinnedRef == "" {
   339	                // No pin available for this action, return original step
   340	                return step
   341	        }
   342	
   343	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Pinning action: %s@%s -> %s", actionRepo, version, pinnedRef)
   344	
   345	        // Create a copy of the step with the pinned reference
   346	        result := step.Clone()
   347	        result.Uses = pinnedRef
   348	
   349	        return result
   350	}
   351	
   352	// extractActionRepo extracts the action repository from a uses string
   353	// For example:
   354	//   - "actions/checkout@v5" -> "actions/checkout"
   355	//   - "actions/setup-node@v6" -> "actions/setup-node"
   356	//   - "github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v3" -> "github/codeql-action/upload-sarif"
   357	//   - "actions/checkout" -> "actions/checkout"
   358	func extractActionRepo(uses string) string {
   359	        // Split on @ to separate repo from version/ref
   360	        before, _, ok := strings.Cut(uses, "@")
   361	        if !ok {
   362	                // No @ found, return the whole string
   363	                return uses
   364	        }
   365	        // Return everything before the @
   366	        return before
   367	}
   368	
   369	// extractActionVersion extracts the version from a uses string
   370	// For example:
   371	//   - "actions/checkout@v5" -> "v4"
   372	//   - "actions/setup-node@v6" -> "v5"
   373	//   - "actions/checkout" -> ""
   374	func extractActionVersion(uses string) string {
   375	        // Split on @ to separate repo from version/ref
   376	        _, after, ok := strings.Cut(uses, "@")
   377	        if !ok {
   378	                // No @ found, no version
   379	                return ""
   380	        }
   381	        // Return everything after the @
   382	        return after
   383	}
   384	
   385	// ApplyActionPinsToTypedSteps applies SHA pinning to a slice of typed WorkflowStep pointers
   386	// Returns a new slice with pinned references - this is the type-safe version
   387	func ApplyActionPinsToTypedSteps(steps []*WorkflowStep, data *WorkflowData) []*WorkflowStep {
   388	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Applying action pins to %d typed steps", len(steps))
   389	        if steps == nil {
   390	                return nil
   391	        }
   392	
   393	        result := make([]*WorkflowStep, 0, len(steps))
   394	        for i, step := range steps {
   395	                if step == nil {
   396	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Skipping nil step at index %d", i)
   397	                        result = append(result, nil)
   398	                        continue
   399	                }
   400	
   401	                pinnedStep := ApplyActionPinToTypedStep(step, data)
   402	                result = append(result, pinnedStep)
   403	        }
   404	
   405	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Successfully applied pins to %d typed steps", len(result))
   406	        return result
   407	}

   409	// GetActionPinByRepo returns the ActionPin for a given repository, if it exists
   410	// When multiple versions exist for the same repo, it returns the latest version by semver
   411	func GetActionPinByRepo(repo string) (ActionPin, bool) {
   412	        actionPins := getActionPins()
   413	
   414	        // Find all pins matching the repo - using functional filter
   415	        matchingPins := sliceutil.Filter(actionPins, func(pin ActionPin) bool {
   416	                return pin.Repo == repo
   417	        })
   418	
   419	        if len(matchingPins) == 0 {
   420	                return ActionPin{}, false
   421	        }
   422	
   423	        // Sort matching pins by version (descending - latest first) - immutable operation
   424	        sortedPins := sortPinsByVersion(matchingPins)
   425	
   426	        // Return the latest version (first after sorting)
   427	        return sortedPins[0], true
   428	}

    16	
    17	// getActionRef returns the action reference string based on action mode and version.
    18	// If a resolver is provided and mode is release or action, attempts to resolve the SHA for a SHA-pinned reference.
    19	// Falls back to a version tag reference if SHA resolution fails or resolver is nil.
    20	func getActionRef(actionMode workflow.ActionMode, version string, resolver workflow.ActionSHAResolver) string {
    21	        if actionMode.IsRelease() && version != "" && version != "dev" {
    22	                if resolver != nil {
    23	                        sha, err := resolver.ResolveSHA("github/gh-aw/actions/setup-cli", version)
    24	                        if err == nil && sha != "" {
    25	                                return fmt.Sprintf("@%s # %s", sha, version)
    26	                        }
    27	                        copilotSetupLog.Printf("Failed to resolve SHA for setup-cli@%s: %v, falling back to version tag", version, err)
    28	                }
    29	                return "@" + version
    30	        }
    31	        if actionMode.IsAction() && version != "" && version != "dev" {
    32	                if resolver != nil {
    33	                        sha, err := resolver.ResolveSHA("github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli", version)
    34	                        if err == nil && sha != "" {
    35	                                return fmt.Sprintf("@%s # %s", sha, version)
    36	                        }
    37	                        copilotSetupLog.Printf("Failed to resolve SHA for gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@%s: %v, falling back to version tag", version, err)
    38	                }
    39	                return "@" + version
    40	        }
    41	        return "@main"
    42	}

    12	
    13	var actionSHACheckerLog = logger.New("workflow:action_sha_checker")
    14	
    15	// actionUsesPattern matches action references in lock files:
    16	// owner/repo@40-char-hex-sha with optional version comment
    17	var actionUsesPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`([a-zA-Z0-9_.-]+/[a-zA-Z0-9_.-]+(?:/[a-zA-Z0-9_.-]+)*)@([0-9a-f]{40})(?:\s*#\s*([^\s]+))?`)
    18	
    19	// ActionUsage represents an action used in a workflow with its SHA
    20	type ActionUsage struct {
    21	        Repo    string // e.g., "actions/checkout"
    22	        SHA     string // The SHA currently used
    23	        Version string // The version tag if available (e.g., "v5")
    24	}
    25	
    26	// ActionUpdateCheck represents the result of checking if an action needs updating
    27	type ActionUpdateCheck struct {
    28	        Action      ActionUsage
    29	        NeedsUpdate bool
    30	        LatestSHA   string
    31	        Message     string
    32	}
    33	
    34	// ExtractActionsFromLockFile parses a lock.yml file and extracts all action usages
    35	func ExtractActionsFromLockFile(lockFilePath string) ([]ActionUsage, error) {
    36	        actionSHACheckerLog.Printf("Extracting actions from lock file: %s", lockFilePath)
    37	
    38	        content, err := os.ReadFile(lockFilePath)
    39	        if err != nil {
    40	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to read lock file: %w", err)
    41	        }
    42	
    43	        // Validate lock file schema compatibility before parsing
    44	        if err := ValidateLockSchemaCompatibility(string(content), lockFilePath); err != nil {
    45	                return nil, err
    46	        }
    47	
    48	        // Parse YAML to extract actions from "uses" fields
    49	        var workflowData map[string]any
    50	        if err := yaml.Unmarshal(content, &workflowData); err != nil {
    51	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse lock file YAML: %w", err)
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        // Convert to string and extract all uses fields
    55	        contentStr := string(content)
    56	        actions := make(map[string]ActionUsage) // Use map to deduplicate
    57	        matches := actionUsesPattern.FindAllStringSubmatch(contentStr, -1)
    58	
    59	        for _, match := range matches {
    60	                if len(match) >= 3 {
    61	                        repo := match[1]
    62	                        sha := match[2]
    63	
    64	                        // Skip if we've already seen this action
    65	                        if _, exists := actions[repo+"@"+sha]; exists {
    66	                                continue
    67	                        }
    68	
    69	                        // Extract version from comment if present (match[3])
    70	                        version := ""
    71	                        if len(match) >= 4 && match[3] != "" {
    72	                                version = match[3]
    73	                                actionSHACheckerLog.Printf("Found action: %s@%s (version: %s)", repo, sha, version)
    74	                        } else {
    75	                                // Fallback: try to determine the version tag from action_pins.json
    76	                                if pin, found := GetActionPinByRepo(repo); found {
    77	                                        version = pin.Version
    78	                                        actionSHACheckerLog.Printf("Found action: %s@%s (version from pins: %s)", repo, sha, version)
    79	                                } else {
    80	                                        actionSHACheckerLog.Printf("Found action: %s@%s (no version)", repo, sha)
    81	                                }
    82	                        }
    83	
    84	                        actions[repo+"@"+sha] = ActionUsage{
    85	                                Repo:    repo,
    86	                                SHA:     sha,
    87	                                Version: version,
    88	                        }
    89	                }
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        // Convert map to slice
    93	        result := make([]ActionUsage, 0, len(actions))
    94	        for _, action := range actions {
    95	                result = append(result, action)
    96	        }
    97	
    98	        actionSHACheckerLog.Printf("Extracted %d unique actions", len(result))
    99	        return result, nil
   100	}
   101	
   102	// CheckActionSHAUpdates checks if actions need updating by comparing with latest SHAs
   103	func CheckActionSHAUpdates(actions []ActionUsage, resolver *ActionResolver) []ActionUpdateCheck {
   104	        actionSHACheckerLog.Printf("Checking %d actions for updates", len(actions))
   105	
   106	        results := make([]ActionUpdateCheck, 0, len(actions))
   107	
   108	        for _, action := range actions {
   109	                check := ActionUpdateCheck{
   110	                        Action:      action,
   111	                        NeedsUpdate: false,
   112	                }
   113	
   114	                // Skip if we don't have a version to check against
   115	                if action.Version == "" {
   116	                        actionSHACheckerLog.Printf("Skipping %s: no version tag available", action.Repo)
   117	                        continue
   118	                }
   119	
   120	                // Resolve the latest SHA for this version
   121	                latestSHA, err := resolver.ResolveSHA(action.Repo, action.Version)
   122	                if err != nil {
   123	                        actionSHACheckerLog.Printf("Failed to resolve %s@%s: %v", action.Repo, action.Version, err)
   124	                        check.Message = fmt.Sprintf("Unable to check for updates: %v", err)
   125	                        results = append(results, check)
   126	                        continue
   127	                }
   128	
   129	                check.LatestSHA = latestSHA
   130	
   131	                // Compare SHAs
   132	                if action.SHA != latestSHA {
   133	                        check.NeedsUpdate = true
   134	                        check.Message = fmt.Sprintf("Action %s@%s is using SHA %s but latest is %s",
   135	                                action.Repo, action.Version, action.SHA[:7], latestSHA[:7])
   136	                        actionSHACheckerLog.Printf("UPDATE NEEDED: %s", check.Message)
   137	                } else {
   138	                        actionSHACheckerLog.Printf("Action %s@%s is up to date", action.Repo, action.Version)
   139	                }
   140

     1	package workflow
     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "context"
     5	        "fmt"
     6	        "strings"
     7	        "time"
     8	
     9	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/gitutil"
    10	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/logger"
    11	)
    12	
    13	var resolverLog = logger.New("workflow:action_resolver")
    14	
    15	// ActionSHAResolver is the minimal interface for resolving an action tag to its commit SHA.
    16	type ActionSHAResolver interface {
    17	        ResolveSHA(repo, version string) (string, error)
    18	}
    19	
    20	// ActionResolver handles resolving action SHAs using GitHub CLI
    21	type ActionResolver struct {
    22	        cache             *ActionCache
    23	        failedResolutions map[string]bool // tracks failed resolution attempts in current run (key: "repo@version")
    24	}
    25	
    26	// NewActionResolver creates a new action resolver
    27	func NewActionResolver(cache *ActionCache) *ActionResolver {
    28	        return &ActionResolver{
    29	                cache:             cache,
    30	                failedResolutions: make(map[string]bool),
    31	        }
    32	}
    33	
    34	// ResolveSHA resolves the SHA for a given action@version using GitHub CLI
    35	// Returns the SHA and an error if resolution fails
    36	func (r *ActionResolver) ResolveSHA(repo, version string) (string, error) {
    37	        resolverLog.Printf("Resolving SHA for action: %s@%s", repo, version)
    38	
    39	        // Create a cache key for tracking failed resolutions
    40	        cacheKey := formatActionCacheKey(repo, version)
    41	
    42	        // Check if we've already failed to resolve this action in this run
    43	        if r.failedResolutions[cacheKey] {
    44	                resolverLog.Printf("Skipping resolution for %s@%s: already failed in this run", repo, version)
    45	                return "", fmt.Errorf("previously failed to resolve %s@%s in this compilation run", repo, version)
    46	        }
    47	
    48	        // Check cache first
    49	        if sha, found := r.cache.Get(repo, version); found {
    50	                resolverLog.Printf("Cache hit for %s@%s: %s", repo, version, sha)
    51	                return sha, nil
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        resolverLog.Printf("Cache miss for %s@%s, querying GitHub API", repo, version)
    55	        resolverLog.Printf("This may take a moment as we query GitHub API at /repos/%s/git/ref/tags/%s", gitutil.ExtractBaseRepo(repo), version)
    56	
    57	        // Resolve using GitHub CLI
    58	        sha, err := r.resolveFromGitHub(repo, version)
    59	        if err != nil {
    60	                resolverLog.Printf("Failed to resolve %s@%s: %v", repo, version, err)
    61	                // Mark this resolution as failed for this compilation run
    62	                r.failedResolutions[cacheKey] = true
    63	                resolverLog.Printf("Marked %s as failed, will not retry in this run", cacheKey)
    64	                return "", err
    65	        }
    66	
    67	        resolverLog.Printf("Successfully resolved %s@%s to SHA: %s", repo, version, sha)
    68	
    69	        // Cache the result
    70	        resolverLog.Printf("Caching result: %s@%s → %s", repo, version, sha)
    71	        r.cache.Set(repo, version, sha)
    72	
    73	        return sha, nil
    74	}
    75	
    76	// resolveFromGitHub uses gh CLI to resolve the SHA for an action@version
    77	func (r *ActionResolver) resolveFromGitHub(repo, version string) (string, error) {
    78	        // Extract base repository (for actions like "github/codeql-action/upload-sarif")
    79	        baseRepo := gitutil.ExtractBaseRepo(repo)
    80	        resolverLog.Printf("Extracted base repository: %s from %s", baseRepo, repo)
    81	
    82	        // Use gh api to get the git ref for the tag
    83	        // API endpoint: GET /repos/{owner}/{repo}/git/ref/tags/{tag}
    84	        apiPath := fmt.Sprintf("/repos/%s/git/ref/tags/%s", baseRepo, version)
    85	        resolverLog.Printf("Querying GitHub API: %s", apiPath)
    86	
    87	        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 20*time.Second)
    88	        defer cancel()
    89	
    90	        cmd := ExecGHContext(ctx, "api", apiPath, "--jq", ".object.sha")
    91	        output, err := cmd.Output()
    92	        if err != nil {
    93	                // Try without "refs/tags/" prefix in case version is already a ref
    94	                return "", fmt.Errorf("failed to resolve %s@%s: %w", repo, version, err)
    95	        }
    96	
    97	        sha := strings.TrimSpace(string(output))
    98	        if sha == "" {
    99	                return "", fmt.Errorf("empty SHA returned for %s@%s", repo, version)
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        // Validate SHA format (should be 40 hex characters)
   103	        if len(sha) != 40 {
   104	                return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid SHA format for %s@%s: %s", repo, version, sha)
   105	        }
   106	
   107	        return sha, nil
   108	}

     1	package workflow
     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "encoding/json"
     5	        "fmt"
     6	        "os"
     7	        "path/filepath"
     8	        "sort"
     9	        "strings"
    10	
    11	        "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/logger"
    12	)
    13	
    14	var actionCacheLog = logger.New("workflow:action_cache")
    15	
    16	const (
    17	        // CacheFileName is the name of the cache file in .github/aw/.
    18	        CacheFileName = "actions-lock.json"
    19	)
    20	
    21	// ActionCacheEntry represents a cached action pin resolution.
    22	type ActionCacheEntry struct {
    23	        Repo              string                      `json:"repo"`
    24	        Version           string                      `json:"version"`
    25	        SHA               string                      `json:"sha"`
    26	        Inputs            map[string]*ActionYAMLInput `json:"inputs,omitempty"`             // cached inputs from action.yml
    27	        ActionDescription string                      `json:"action_description,omitempty"` // cached description from action.yml
    28	}
    29	
    30	// ActionCache manages cached action pin resolutions.
    31	type ActionCache struct {
    32	        Entries map[string]ActionCacheEntry `json:"entries"` // key: "repo@version"
    33	        path    string
    34	        dirty   bool // tracks if cache has unsaved changes
    35	}
    36	
    37	// NewActionCache creates a new action cache instance
    38	func NewActionCache(repoRoot string) *ActionCache {
    39	        cachePath := filepath.Join(repoRoot, ".github", "aw", CacheFileName)
    40	        actionCacheLog.Printf("Creating action cache with path: %s", cachePath)
    41	        return &ActionCache{
    42	                Entries: make(map[string]ActionCacheEntry),
    43	                path:    cachePath,
    44	                // dirty is initialized to false (zero value)
    45	        }
    46	}
    47	
    48	// Load loads the cache from disk
    49	func (c *ActionCache) Load() error {
    50	        actionCacheLog.Printf("Loading action cache from: %s", c.path)
    51	        data, err := os.ReadFile(c.path)
    52	        if err != nil {
    53	                if os.IsNotExist(err) {
    54	                        // Cache file doesn't exist yet, that's OK
    55	                        actionCacheLog.Print("Cache file does not exist, starting with empty cache")
    56	                        return nil
    57	                }
    58	                actionCacheLog.Printf("Failed to read cache file: %v", err)
    59	                return err
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        if err := json.Unmarshal(data, c); err != nil {
    63	                actionCacheLog.Printf("Failed to unmarshal cache data: %v", err)
    64	                return err
    65	        }
    66	
    67	        // Mark cache as clean after successful load (it matches disk state)
    68	        c.dirty = false
    69	
    70	        actionCacheLog.Printf("Successfully loaded cache with %d entries", len(c.Entries))
    71	        return nil
    72	}
    73	
    74	// Save saves the cache to disk with sorted entries
    75	// If the cache is empty, the file is not created or is deleted if it exists
    76	// Deduplicates entries by keeping only the most precise version reference for each repo+SHA combination
    77	// Only saves if the cache has been modified (dirty flag is true)
    78	func (c *ActionCache) Save() error {
    79	        // Skip saving if cache hasn't been modified
    80	        if !c.dirty {
    81	                actionCacheLog.Printf("Cache is clean (no changes), skipping save")
    82	                return nil
    83	        }
    84	
    85	        actionCacheLog.Printf("Saving action cache to: %s with %d entries", c.path, len(c.Entries))
    86	
    87	        // If cache is empty, skip saving and delete the file if it exists
    88	        if len(c.Entries) == 0 {
    89	                actionCacheLog.Print("Cache is empty, skipping file creation")
    90	                // Remove the file if it exists
    91	                if _, err := os.Stat(c.path); err == nil {
    92	                        actionCacheLog.Printf("Removing existing empty cache file: %s", c.path)
    93	                        if err := os.Remove(c.path); err != nil {
    94	                                actionCacheLog.Printf("Failed to remove empty cache file: %v", err)
    95	                                return err
    96	                        }
    97	                }
    98	                c.dirty = false
    99	                return nil
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        // Deduplicate entries before saving
   103	        c.deduplicateEntries()
   104	
   105	        // Ensure directory exists
   106	        dir := filepath.Dir(c.path)
   107	        if err := os.MkdirAll(dir, 0755); err != nil {
   108	                actionCacheLog.Printf("Failed to create cache directory: %v", err)
   109	                return err
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        // Marshal with sorted entries
   113	        data, err := c.marshalSorted()
   114	        if err != nil {
   115	                actionCacheLog.Printf("Failed to marshal cache data: %v", err)
   116	                return err
   117	        }
   118	
   119	        // Add trailing newline for prettier compliance
   120	        data = append(data, '\n')
   121	
   122	        if err := os.WriteFile(c.path, data, 0644); err != nil {
   123	                actionCacheLog.Printf("Failed to write cache file: %v", err)
   124	                return err
   125	        }
   126	
   127	        actionCacheLog.Print("Successfully saved action cache")
   128	        c.dirty = false
   129	        return nil
   130	}
   131	
   132	// marshalSorted marshals the cache with entries sorted by key
   133	func (c *ActionCache) marshalSorted() ([]byte, error) {
   134	        // Extract and sort the keys
   135	        keys := make([]string, 0, len(c.Entries))
   136	        for key := range c.Entries {
   137	                keys = append(keys, key)
   138	        }
   139	        sort.Strings(keys)
   140	
   141	        // Manually construct JSON with sorted keys
   142	        var result []byte
   143	        result = append(result, []byte("{\n  \"entries\": {\n")...)
   144	
   145	        for i, key := range keys {
   146	                entry := c.Entries[key]
   147	
   148	                // Marshal the entry
   149	                entryJSON, err := json.MarshalIndent(entry, "    ", "  ")
   150	                if err != nil {
   151	                        return nil, err
   152	                }
   153	
   154	                // Add the key and entry
   155	                result = append(result, []byte("    \""+key+"\": ")...)
   156	                result = append(result, entryJSON...)
   157	
   158	                // Add comma if not the last entry
   159	                if i < len(keys)-1 {
   160	                        result = append(result, ',')
   161	                }
   162	                result = append(result, '\n')
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        result = append(result, []byte("  }\n}")...)
   166	        return result, nil
   167	}
   168	
   169	// Delete removes the cache entry for the given repo and version.
   170	// It first tries the canonical formatted key, then falls back to scanning all
   171	// entries for a matching repo+version pair to handle key/version mismatches.
   172	// It is a no-op if no matching entry is found.
   173	func (c *ActionCache) Delete(repo, version string) {
   174	        key := formatActionCacheKey(repo, version)
   175	
   176	        deleted := false
   177	
   178	        // First, try deleting by the canonical formatted key.
   179	        if _, exists := c.Entries[key]; exists {
   180	                delete(c.Entries, key)

   215	        key := formatActionCacheKey(repo, version)

   229	        for key, entry := range c.Entries {

   238	// Set stores a new cache entry, preserving any already-cached inputs when the SHA
   239	// is unchanged. If the SHA changes (e.g. a moving tag points to a new commit),
   240	// cached inputs are cleared to stay consistent with the newly-pinned commit.
   241	func (c *ActionCache) Set(repo, version, sha string) {
   242	        key := formatActionCacheKey(repo, version)
   243	
   244	        // Check if there are existing entries with the same repo+SHA but different version
   245	        for existingKey, entry := range c.Entries {
   246	                if entry.Repo == repo && entry.SHA == sha && entry.Version != version {
   247	                        // Truncate SHA for logging (handle short SHAs in tests)
   248	                        shortSHA := sha
   249	                        if len(sha) > 8 {
   250	                                shortSHA = sha[:8]
   251	                        }
   252	                        actionCacheLog.Printf("WARNING: Adding cache entry %s with SHA %s that already exists as %s",
   253	                                key, shortSHA, existingKey)
   254	                        actionCacheLog.Printf("This may cause version comment flipping in lock files. Consider using consistent version tags.")
   255	                }
   256	        }
   257	
   258	        actionCacheLog.Printf("Setting cache entry: key=%s, sha=%s", key, sha)
   259	
   260	        // Preserve previously-cached inputs only when the SHA is unchanged. If the SHA
   261	        // changes (e.g. for a moving tag that now points to a new commit), drop any
   262	        // existing inputs so they stay consistent with the pinned commit.
   263	        existing := c.Entries[key]
   264	        var inputs map[string]*ActionYAMLInput
   265	        var description string
   266	        if existing.SHA == sha {
   267	                inputs = existing.Inputs
   268	                description = existing.ActionDescription
   269	        } else if existing.SHA != "" {
   270	                // Log when an existing entry's SHA is being changed (covers both the case
   271	                // where cached inputs exist and where they don't, for consistent observability).
   272	                actionCacheLog.Printf("Clearing cached inputs for key=%s due to SHA change (%s -> %s)", key, existing.SHA, sha)
   273	        }
   274	        c.Entries[key] = ActionCacheEntry{
   275	                Repo:              repo,
   276	                Version:           version,
   277	                SHA:               sha,
   278	                Inputs:            inputs,
   279	                ActionDescription: description,
   280	        }
   281	        c.dirty = true // Mark cache as modified
   282	}

   284	// GetInputs retrieves the cached action inputs for the given repo and version.
   285	// Returns the inputs map and true if cached inputs exist, otherwise nil and false.
   286	func (c *ActionCache) GetInputs(repo, version string) (map[string]*ActionYAMLInput, bool) {
   287	        key := formatActionCacheKey(repo, version)
   288	        entry, exists := c.Entries[key]
   289	        if !exists || entry.Inputs == nil {
   290	                actionCacheLog.Printf("No cached inputs for key=%s", key)
   291	                return nil, false
   292	        }
   293	        actionCacheLog.Printf("Cache hit for inputs: key=%s, inputs=%d", key, len(entry.Inputs))
   294	        return entry.Inputs, true
   295	}

   297	// SetInputs stores the action inputs in the cache entry for the given repo and version.
   298	// If no cache entry exists for the key, a new entry is created with an empty SHA so that
   299	// inputs fetched from the network are persisted even before the SHA is resolved.
   300	func (c *ActionCache) SetInputs(repo, version string, inputs map[string]*ActionYAMLInput) {
   301	        key := formatActionCacheKey(repo, version)
   302	        entry, exists := c.Entries[key]
   303	        if !exists {
   304	                actionCacheLog.Printf("No cache entry for key=%s, creating new entry to store inputs", key)
   305	                entry = ActionCacheEntry{
   306	                        Repo:    repo,
   307	                        Version: version,
   308	                }
   309	        }
   310	        entry.Inputs = inputs
   311	        c.Entries[key] = entry
   312	        c.dirty = true
   313	        actionCacheLog.Printf("Cached inputs for key=%s, inputs=%d", key, len(inputs))
   314	}

   316	// GetActionDescription retrieves the cached action description for the given repo and version.
   317	// Returns the description and true if a non-empty description is cached, otherwise "" and false.
   318	func (c *ActionCache) GetActionDescription(repo, version string) (string, bool) {
   319	        key := formatActionCacheKey(repo, version)
   320	        entry, exists := c.Entries[key]
   321	        if !exists || entry.ActionDescription == "" {
   322	                return "", false
   323	        }
   324	        return entry.ActionDescription, true
   325	}
   326	
   327	// SetActionDescription stores the action description in the cache entry for the given repo and version.
   328	// If no cache entry exists for the key, a new entry is created.
   329	// Empty descriptions are not stored; actions without a description string are treated the same as
   330	// actions whose description has not yet been fetched, so we avoid caching an empty string that
   331	// would prevent a later fetch from populating the field.
   332	func (c *ActionCache) SetActionDescription(repo, version, description string) {
   333	        if description == "" {
   334	                // Skip persisting empty descriptions; callers that want to distinguish
   335	                // "no description fetched" from "action has no description" should use
   336	                // a sentinel value. For our use case (action.yml display text), omitting
   337	                // empty values is intentional to keep the cache file tidy.
   338	                return
   339	        }
   340	        key := formatActionCacheKey(repo, version)
   341	        entry, exists := c.Entries[key]
   342	        if !exists {
   343	                entry = ActionCacheEntry{
   344	                        Repo:    repo,
   345	                        Version: version,
   346	                }
   347	        }
   348	        entry.ActionDescription = description
   349	        c.Entries[key] = entry
   350	        c.dirty = true
   351	        actionCacheLog.Printf("Cached description for key=%s", key)
   352	}

/testbed/pkg/workflow/action_reference.go:37:func ResolveSetupActionReference(actionMode ActionMode, version string, actionTag string, resolver ActionSHAResolver) string {
package workflow

import (
	"fmt"
	"strings"

	"github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/logger"
)

var actionRefLog = logger.New("workflow:action_reference")

const (
	// GitHubOrgRepo is the organization and repository name for custom action references
	GitHubOrgRepo = "github/gh-aw"

	// GitHubActionsOrgRepo is the organization and repository name for the external gh-aw-actions repository
	GitHubActionsOrgRepo = "github/gh-aw-actions"
)

// ResolveSetupActionReference resolves the actions/setup action reference based on action mode and version.
// This is a standalone helper function that can be used by both Compiler methods and standalone
// workflow generators (like maintenance workflow) that don't have access to WorkflowData.
//
// Parameters:
//   - actionMode: The action mode (dev, release, or action)
//   - version: The version string to use for release/action mode
//   - actionTag: Optional override tag/SHA (takes precedence over version when in release mode)
//   - resolver: Optional ActionSHAResolver for dynamic SHA resolution (can be nil for standalone use)
//
// Returns:
//   - For dev mode: "./actions/setup" (local path)
//   - For release mode with resolver: "github/gh-aw/actions/setup@<sha> # <version>" (SHA-pinned)
//   - For release mode without resolver: "github/gh-aw/actions/setup@<version>" (tag-based, SHA resolved later)
//   - For action mode with resolver: "github/gh-aw-actions/setup@<sha> # <version>" (SHA-pinned)
//   - For action mode without resolver: "github/gh-aw-actions/setup@<version>" (tag-based, SHA resolved later)
//   - Falls back to local path if version is invalid in release/action mode
func ResolveSetupActionReference(actionMode ActionMode, version string, actionTag string, resolver ActionSHAResolver) string {
	return resolveSetupActionRef(actionMode, version, actionTag, resolver, "")
}

// resolveSetupActionRef is the internal implementation of ResolveSetupActionReference
// that accepts an optional actionsOrgRepo override. When actionsOrgRepo is empty,
// GitHubActionsOrgRepo is used.
func resolveSetupActionRef(actionMode ActionMode, version string, actionTag string, resolver ActionSHAResolver, actionsOrgRepo string) string {
	if actionsOrgRepo == "" {
		actionsOrgRepo = GitHubActionsOrgRepo
	}

	localPath := "./actions/setup"

	// Dev mode - return local path
	if actionMode == ActionModeDev {
		actionRefLog.Printf("Dev mode: using local action path: %s", localPath)
		return localPath
	}

	// Action mode - use external gh-aw-actions repository with SHA pinning if possible
	if actionMode == ActionModeAction {
		// Use actionTag if provided, otherwise fall back to version
		tag := actionTag
		if tag == "" {
			tag = version
		}

		// Check if tag is valid for action mode
		if tag == "" || tag == "dev" {
			actionRefLog.Print("WARNING: No release tag available in binary version (version is 'dev' or empty), falling back to local path")
			return localPath
		}

		// Construct the remote reference: <actionsOrgRepo>/setup@tag
		actionRepo := actionsOrgRepo + "/setup"
		remoteRef := fmt.Sprintf("%s@%s", actionRepo, tag)

		// If a resolver is available, try to resolve the SHA
		if resolver != nil {
			sha, err := resolver.ResolveSHA(actionRepo, tag)
			if err == nil && sha != "" {
				pinnedRef := formatActionReference(actionRepo, sha, tag)
				actionRefLog.Printf("Action mode: resolved %s to SHA-pinned reference: %s", remoteRef, pinnedRef)
				return pinnedRef
			}
			if err != nil {
				actionRefLog.Printf("Failed to resolve SHA for %s@%s: %v", actionRepo, tag, err)
			}
		}

		// If no resolver or SHA resolution failed, return tag-based reference
		actionRefLog.Printf("Action mode: using tag-based external actions repo reference: %s (SHA will be resolved later)", remoteRef)
		return remoteRef
	}

	// Release mode - convert to remote reference
	if actionMode == ActionModeRelease {
		actionPath := strings.TrimPrefix(localPath, "./")

		// Use actionTag if provided, otherwise fall back to version
		tag := actionTag
		if tag == "" {
			tag = version
		}

		// Check if tag is valid for release mode
		if tag == "" || tag == "dev" {
			actionRefLog.Print("WARNING: No release tag available in binary version (version is 'dev' or empty), falling back to local path")
			return localPath
		}

		// Construct the remote reference with tag: github/gh-aw/actions/setup@tag
		actionRepo := fmt.Sprintf("%s/%s", GitHubOrgRepo, actionPath)
		remoteRef := fmt.Sprintf("%s@%s", actionRepo, tag)

		// If a resolver is available, try to resolve the SHA
		if resolver != nil {
			sha, err := resolver.ResolveSHA(actionRepo, tag)
			if err == nil && sha != "" {
				pinnedRef := formatActionReference(actionRepo, sha, tag)
				actionRefLog.Printf("Release mode: resolved %s to SHA-pinned reference: %s", remoteRef, pinnedRef)
				return pinnedRef
			}

   137	// resolveActionReference converts a local action path to the appropriate reference
   138	// based on the current action mode (dev vs release vs action).
   139	// If action-tag is specified in features, it overrides the mode check and enables action mode behavior
   140	// (using the github/gh-aw-actions external repository).
   141	// For dev mode: returns the local path as-is (e.g., "./actions/create-issue")
   142	// For release mode: converts to SHA-pinned remote reference (e.g., "github/gh-aw/actions/create-issue@SHA # tag")
   143	// For action mode: converts to SHA-pinned reference in external repo if possible (e.g., "github/gh-aw-actions/create-issue@SHA # version")
   144	func (c *Compiler) resolveActionReference(localActionPath string, data *WorkflowData) string {
   145	        // Check if action-tag is specified in features - if so, override mode and use action mode behavior
   146	        hasActionTag := false
   147	        var frontmatterActionTag string
   148	        if data != nil && data.Features != nil {
   149	                if actionTagVal, exists := data.Features["action-tag"]; exists {
   150	                        if actionTagStr, ok := actionTagVal.(string); ok && actionTagStr != "" {
   151	                                hasActionTag = true
   152	                                frontmatterActionTag = actionTagStr
   153	                                actionRefLog.Printf("action-tag feature detected: %s - using action mode behavior", actionTagStr)
   154	                        }
   155	                }
   156	        }
   157	
   158	        // For ./actions/setup, check for compiler-level actionTag override first
   159	        if localActionPath == "./actions/setup" {
   160	                // Use compiler actionTag if available, otherwise check features
   161	                var resolver ActionSHAResolver
   162	                if data != nil && data.ActionResolver != nil {
   163	                        resolver = data.ActionResolver
   164	                }
   165	                if c.actionTag != "" {
   166	                        return resolveSetupActionRef(c.actionMode, c.version, c.actionTag, resolver, c.effectiveActionsRepo())
   167	                }
   168	                if !hasActionTag {
   169	                        return resolveSetupActionRef(c.actionMode, c.version, "", resolver, c.effectiveActionsRepo())
   170	                }
   171	                // hasActionTag is true and no compiler actionTag: use action mode with the frontmatter tag
   172	                return resolveSetupActionRef(ActionModeAction, c.version, frontmatterActionTag, resolver, c.effectiveActionsRepo())
   173	        }
   174	
   175	        // Action mode - use external gh-aw-actions repository
   176	        if c.actionMode == ActionModeAction || hasActionTag {
   177	                return c.convertToExternalActionsRef(localActionPath, data)
   178	        }
   179	
   180	        // Use release mode
   181	        if c.actionMode == ActionModeRelease {
   182	                // Convert to tag-based remote reference for release
   183	                remoteRef := c.convertToRemoteActionRef(localActionPath, data)
   184	                if remoteRef == "" {
   185	                        actionRefLog.Printf("WARNING: Could not resolve remote reference for %s", localActionPath)
   186	                        return ""
   187	                }
   188	
   189	                // Now resolve the tag to a SHA using action pins
   190	                // Extract repo and version from the remote reference (format: "repo/path@version")
   191	                actionRepo := extractActionRepo(remoteRef)
   192	                version := extractActionVersion(remoteRef)
   193	
   194	                if actionRepo != "" && version != "" {
   195	                        // Resolve the SHA using action pins
   196	                        pinnedRef, err := GetActionPinWithData(actionRepo, version, data)
   197	                        if err != nil {
   198	                                // In strict mode, GetActionPinWithData returns an error
   199	                                actionRefLog.Printf("Failed to pin action %s@%s: %v", actionRepo, version, err)
   200	                                return ""
   201	                        }
   202	                        if pinnedRef != "" {
   203	                                // Successfully resolved to SHA
   204	                                actionRefLog.Printf("Release mode: resolved %s to SHA-pinned reference: %s", remoteRef, pinnedRef)
   205	                                return pinnedRef
   206	                        }
   207	                }
   208	
   209	                // If we couldn't resolve to SHA, return the tag-based reference
   210	                // This happens in non-strict mode when no pin is available
   211	                actionRefLog.Printf("Release mode: using tag-based remote action reference: %s", remoteRef)
   212	                return remoteRef
   213	        }
   214	
   215	        // Dev mode - return local path
   216	        if c.actionMode == ActionModeDev {
   217	                actionRefLog.Printf("Dev mode: using local action path: %s", localActionPath)
   218	                return localActionPath
   219	        }
   220	
   221	        // Default to dev mode for unknown modes
   222	        actionRefLog.Printf("WARNING: Unknown action mode %s, defaulting to dev mode", c.actionMode)
   223	        return localActionPath
   224	}
   225	
   226	// convertToRemoteActionRef converts a local action path to a tag-based remote reference
   227	// that will be resolved to a SHA later in the release pipeline using action pins.
   228	// Uses the action-tag from WorkflowData.Features if specified (for testing), otherwise uses the version stored in the compiler binary.
   229	// If compiler has actionTag set, it takes priority over both.
   230	// Example: "./actions/create-issue" -> "github/gh-aw/actions/create-issue@v1.0.0"

package main
import (
  "fmt"
  "os"
  "path/filepath"
  "strings"
  "github.com/github/gh-aw/pkg/workflow"
)
func main() {
  dir, err := os.MkdirTemp("", "gh-aw-maint-repro-")
  if err != nil { panic(err) }
  defer os.RemoveAll(dir)
  data := []*workflow.WorkflowData{{
    Name: "test-workflow",
    SafeOutputs: &workflow.SafeOutputsConfig{CreateIssues: &workflow.CreateIssuesConfig{Expires: 48}},
  }}
  if err := workflow.GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow(data, dir, "v0.64.0", workflow.ActionModeAction, "", false); err != nil { panic(err) }
  content, err := os.ReadFile(filepath.Join(dir, "agentics-maintenance.yml"))
  if err != nil { panic(err) }
  s := string(content)
  bad := "uses: github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@v0.64.0"
  good := "uses: github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@51c65948c64ab6752536ead71fba1fc2c20ed0bc # v0.64.0"
  if strings.Contains(s, bad) && !strings.Contains(s, good) {
    fmt.Println("BUG: setup-cli is referenced by mutable tag")
    for _, line := range strings.Split(s, "\n") {
      if strings.Contains(line, "setup-cli@") { fmt.Println(line) }
    }
    os.Exit(1)
  }
  if !strings.Contains(s, good) {
    fmt.Println("BUG: expected pinned setup-cli reference not found")
    for _, line := range strings.Split(s, "\n") {
      if strings.Contains(line, "setup-cli@") { fmt.Println(line) }
    }
    os.Exit(1)
  }
  fmt.Println("OK: setup-cli reference is SHA-pinned")
}
GO

    11	
    12	// ActionMode defines how JavaScript is embedded in workflow steps
    13	type ActionMode string
    14	
    15	const (
    16	        // ActionModeDev references custom actions using local paths (development mode, default)
    17	        ActionModeDev ActionMode = "dev"
    18	
    19	        // ActionModeRelease references custom actions using SHA-pinned remote paths (release mode)
    20	        ActionModeRelease ActionMode = "release"
    21	
    22	        // ActionModeScript runs setup.sh script from checked-out .github folder instead of using action steps
    23	        ActionModeScript ActionMode = "script"
    24	
    25	        // ActionModeAction references custom actions from the github/gh-aw-actions repository using the same release version
    26	        ActionModeAction ActionMode = "action"
    27	)
    28	
    29	// String returns the string representation of the action mode
    30	func (m ActionMode) String() string {
    31	        return string(m)
    32	}
    33	
    34	// IsValid checks if the action mode is valid
    35	func (m ActionMode) IsValid() bool {
    36	        return m == ActionModeDev || m == ActionModeRelease || m == ActionModeScript || m == ActionModeAction
    37	}
    38	
    39	// IsDev returns true if the action mode is development mode
    40	func (m ActionMode) IsDev() bool {
    41	        return m == ActionModeDev
    42	}
    43	
    44	// IsRelease returns true if the action mode is release mode
    45	func (m ActionMode) IsRelease() bool {
    46	        return m == ActionModeRelease
    47	}

    50	func (m ActionMode) IsScript() bool {
    51	        return m == ActionModeScript
    52	}

    54	// IsAction returns true if the action mode is action mode (uses github/gh-aw-actions repo)

    56	        return m == ActionModeAction
    57	}
    58	
    59	// UsesExternalActions returns true (always true since inline mode was removed)
    60	func (m ActionMode) UsesExternalActions() bool {
    61	        return true
    62	}
    63	
    64	// DetectActionMode determines the appropriate action mode based on the release flag.
    65	// Returns ActionModeAction if this binary was built as a release (controlled by the
    66	// isReleaseBuild flag set via -X linker flag at build time), or when running in a
    67	// GitHub Actions release context (release tags, release branches, or release events).
    68	// Returns ActionModeDev for all other cases (PRs, feature branches, local development).
    69	// Can be overridden with GH_AW_ACTION_MODE environment variable.
    70	// The version parameter is kept for backward compatibility but is no longer used for detection.
    71	func DetectActionMode(version string) ActionMode {
    72	        actionModeLog.Printf("Detecting action mode: version=%s, isRelease=%v", version, IsRelease())
    73	
    74	        // Check for explicit override via environment variable
    75	        if envMode := os.Getenv("GH_AW_ACTION_MODE"); envMode != "" {
    76	                mode := ActionMode(envMode)
    77	                if mode.IsValid() {
    78	                        actionModeLog.Printf("Using action mode from environment override: %s", mode)
    79	                        return mode
    80	                }
    81	                actionModeLog.Printf("Invalid action mode in environment: %s, falling back to auto-detection", envMode)
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        // Check if this binary was built as a release using the release flag
    85	        // This flag is set at build time via -X linker flag and does not rely on version string heuristics
    86	        if IsRelease() {
    87	                actionModeLog.Printf("Detected action mode from build flag (isReleaseBuild=true)")
    88	                return ActionModeAction
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        // Check GitHub Actions context for additional hints
    92	        githubRef := os.Getenv("GITHUB_REF")
    93	        githubEventName := os.Getenv("GITHUB_EVENT_NAME")
    94	        actionModeLog.Printf("GitHub context: ref=%s, event=%s", githubRef, githubEventName)
    95	
    96	        // Conditions that return ActionModeAction from GitHub Actions context:
    97	        // 1. Running on a release branch (refs/heads/release*)
    98	        // 2. Running on a release tag (refs/tags/*)
    99	        // 3. Running on a release event
   100	        if strings.HasPrefix(githubRef, "refs/heads/release") ||
   101	                strings.HasPrefix(githubRef, "refs/tags/") ||
   102	                githubEventName == "release" {
   103	                actionModeLog.Printf("Detected action mode from GitHub context: ref=%s, event=%s", githubRef, githubEventName)
   104	                return ActionModeAction
   105	        }
   106	
   107	        // Default to dev mode for all other cases:
   108	        // 1. Running on a PR (refs/pull/*)
   109	        // 2. Running locally (no GITHUB_REF)
   110	        // 3. Running on any other branch (including main)
   111	        // 4. Non-release builds (isReleaseBuild=false)
   112	        actionModeLog.Printf("Detected dev mode (default): isRelease=%v, ref=%s", IsRelease(), githubRef)
   113	        return ActionModeDev
   114	}
   115	
   116	// GetActionModeFromWorkflowData extracts the ActionMode from WorkflowData, defaulting to dev mode if nil
   117	func GetActionModeFromWorkflowData(workflowData *WorkflowData) ActionMode {
   118	        if workflowData != nil {
   119	                return workflowData.ActionMode
   120	        }
   121	        return ActionModeDev
   122	}
   123

' --new_str '// generateInstallCLISteps generates YAML steps to install or build the gh-aw CLI.
// In dev mode: builds from source using Setup Go + Build gh-aw (./gh-aw binary available)
// In release mode: installs the released CLI via the setup-cli action (gh aw available)
// In action mode: installs the released CLI via the gh-aw-actions/setup-cli action (gh aw available)
func generateInstallCLISteps(actionMode ActionMode, version string, actionTag string) string {
        return generateInstallCLIStepsWithResolver(actionMode, version, actionTag, nil)
}

// generateInstallCLIStepsWithResolver is like generateInstallCLISteps, but can use
// the compiler'"'"'s action resolver/cache to SHA-pin the setup-cli action reference.
func generateInstallCLIStepsWithResolver(actionMode ActionMode, version string, actionTag string, resolver ActionSHAResolver) string {
        if actionMode == ActionModeDev {
                return `      - name: Setup Go
        uses: ` + GetActionPin("actions/setup-go") + `
        with:
          go-version-file: go.mod
          cache: true

      - name: Build gh-aw
        run: make build

`
        }

        cliTag := actionTag
        if cliTag == "" {
                cliTag = version
        }

        actionRef := resolveSetupCLIActionReference(actionMode, cliTag, resolver)

        return `      - name: Install gh-aw
        uses: ` + actionRef + `
        with:
          version: ` + cliTag + `

`
}

// resolveSetupCLIActionReference returns the setup-cli action reference for the
// selected mode, preferring a full commit SHA from the resolver/cache and then
// falling back to the embedded action pins. If no pin is available, it preserves
// the historical tag-based reference.
func resolveSetupCLIActionReference(actionMode ActionMode, tag string, resolver ActionSHAResolver) string {
        actionRepo := "github/gh-aw/actions/setup-cli"
        if actionMode == ActionModeAction {
                actionRepo = "github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli"
        }

        if isValidFullSHA(tag) {
                return formatActionReference(actionRepo, tag, tag)
        }

        if resolver != nil {
                if sha, err := resolver.ResolveSHA(actionRepo, tag); err == nil && sha != "" {
                        return formatActionReference(actionRepo, sha, tag)
                } else if err != nil {
                        maintenanceLog.Printf("Failed to resolve SHA for %s@%s: %v", actionRepo, tag, err)
                }
        }

        if pinnedRef, found := GetActionPinForVersion(actionRepo, tag); found {
                return pinnedRef
        }

        return actionRepo + "@" + tag
}

// GetActionPinForVersion returns the pinned action reference for a specific
// action repository and version, if the embedded action pins contain an exact
// match. The returned reference includes a comment with the requested version
// tag (e.g., "repo@sha # v1").
func GetActionPinForVersion(actionRepo, version string) (string, bool) {
        actionPins := getActionPins()

        for _, pin := range actionPins {
                if pin.Repo == actionRepo && pin.Version == version {
                        return formatActionReference(actionRepo, pin.SHA, pin.Version), true
                }
        }

        return "", false
}

   130	        return result

   132	
   133	// GetActionPin returns the pinned action reference for a given action repository
   134	// When multiple versions exist for the same repo, it returns the latest version by semver
   135	// If no pin is found, it returns an empty string
   136	// The returned reference includes a comment with the version tag (e.g., "repo@sha # v1")
   137	func GetActionPin(actionRepo string) string {
   138	        actionPins := getActionPins()
   139	
   140	        // Find all pins matching the repo - using functional filter
   141	        matchingPins := sliceutil.Filter(actionPins, func(pin ActionPin) bool {
   142	                return pin.Repo == actionRepo
   143	        })
   144	
   145	        if len(matchingPins) == 0 {
   146	                // If no pin exists, return empty string to signal that this action is not pinned
   147	                return ""
   148	        }
   149	
   150	        // Sort matching pins by version (descending - latest first) - immutable operation
   151	        sortedPins := sortPinsByVersion(matchingPins)
   152	
   153	        // Return the latest version (first after sorting)
   154	        latestPin := sortedPins[0]
   155	        return formatActionReference(actionRepo, latestPin.SHA, latestPin.Version)
   156	}
   157	
   158	// GetActionPinForVersion returns the pinned action reference for a specific
   159	// action repository and version, if the embedded action pins contain an exact
   160	// match. The returned reference includes a comment with the requested version
   161	// tag (e.g., "repo@sha # v1").

+// GetActionPinForVersion returns the pinned action reference for a specific
+// action repository and version, if the embedded action pins contain an exact
+// match. The returned reference includes a comment with the requested version
+// tag (e.g., "repo@sha # v1").
+func GetActionPinForVersion(actionRepo, version string) (string, bool) {
+	actionPins := getActionPins()

diff --git a/testbin/gh b/testbin/gh
new file mode 100755
index 0000000..b2c595a

@@ -0,0 +1,60 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env bash
+set -euo pipefail
+
+cmd="${1:-}"
+shift || true
+
+case "$cmd" in
+  run)
+    sub="${1:-}"
+    shift || true
+    if [ "$sub" = "list" ]; then
+      echo "[]"
+      exit 0
+    fi
+    if [ "$sub" = "view" ]; then
+      echo "could not get workflow run: HTTP 404: Not Found (https://api.github.com/repos/owner/repo/actions/runs/12345)" >&2
+      exit 1
+    fi
+    ;;
+  workflow)
+    sub="${1:-}"
+    shift || true
+    if [ "$sub" = "list" ]; then
+      repo=""
+      args=("$@")
+      for ((i=0; i<${#args[@]}; i++)); do
+        if [ "${args[$i]}" = "--repo" ] && [ $((i+1)) -lt ${#args[@]} ]; then
+          repo="${args[$((i+1))]}"
+        fi
+      done
+      if [ "$repo" = "owner/repo" ]; then
+        echo "could not get workflows: HTTP 404: Not Found (https://api.github.com/repos/owner/repo/actions/workflows?per_page=50&page=1)" >&2
+        exit 1
+      fi
+      echo "[]"
+      exit 0
+    fi
+    ;;
+  pr)
+    sub="${1:-}"
+    shift || true
+    if [ "$sub" = "list" ]; then
+      echo "[]"
+      exit 0
+    fi
+    ;;
+  api)
+    echo "{}"
+    exit 0
+    ;;
+  auth)
+    sub="${1:-}"
+    if [ "$sub" = "status" ]; then
+      echo "You are not logged into any GitHub hosts. Run gh auth login." >&2
+      exit 1
+    fi
+    ;;
+esac
+
+echo "[]"

</diff>

+// GetActionPinForVersion returns the pinned action reference for a specific
+// action repository and version, if the embedded action pins contain an exact
+// match. The returned reference includes a comment with the requested version
+// tag (e.g., "repo@sha # v1").
+func GetActionPinForVersion(actionRepo, version string) (string, bool) {
+	actionPins := getActionPins()
+
+	for _, pin := range actionPins {
+		if pin.Repo == actionRepo && pin.Version == version {
+			return formatActionReference(actionRepo, pin.SHA, pin.Version), true
+		}
+	}
+
+	return "", false
+}
+

 // It tries dynamic resolution first, then falls back to hardcoded pins
 // If resolution fails, emits a warning and returns empty string (in both strict and non-strict modes)

+// resolveSetupCLIActionReference returns the setup-cli action reference for the
+// selected mode, preferring a full commit SHA from the resolver/cache and then
+// falling back to the embedded action pins. If no pin is available, it preserves
+// the historical tag-based reference.
+func resolveSetupCLIActionReference(actionMode ActionMode, tag string, resolver ActionSHAResolver) string {
+	actionRepo := "github/gh-aw/actions/setup-cli"
+	if actionMode == ActionModeAction {
+		actionRepo = "github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli"
 	}
 
-	// Release mode: use setup-cli action (consistent with copilot-setup-steps.yml)
-	return `      - name: Install gh-aw
-        uses: github/gh-aw/actions/setup-cli@` + cliTag + `
-        with:
-          version: ` + cliTag + `
+	if isValidFullSHA(tag) {
+		return formatActionReference(actionRepo, tag, tag)
+	}
 
-`
+	if resolver != nil {
+		if sha, err := resolver.ResolveSHA(actionRepo, tag); err == nil && sha != "" {
+			return formatActionReference(actionRepo, sha, tag)
+		} else if err != nil {
+			maintenanceLog.Printf("Failed to resolve SHA for %s@%s: %v", actionRepo, tag, err)
+		}
+	}
+
+	if pinnedRef, found := GetActionPinForVersion(actionRepo, tag); found {
+		return pinnedRef
+	}
+
+	return actionRepo + "@" + tag
 }
